The law establishes that employee monitoring through cameras requires compliance with the GDPR and LOPDGDD, with specific limitations on scope and retention.\n\n## Consent Requirements for Employee Data\n\n**Article 6** specifies that consent must be \"free, specific, informed and unequivocal\" and cannot be obtained through silence or inactivity. For multiple purposes, consent requirements state: *\"consent must be given in a specific and unequivocal manner for all of them\"* (Article 6.2).\n\nCritically, **Article 6.3** prohibits conditioning contract performance on unrelated data processing consents.\n\n## Gamification & Scoring Systems\n\nThe law does not explicitly address gamification scores. The statute specifies that \"treatment of information shall be subject to principles and guarantees established in applicable data protection regulations.\"\n\nWorker representatives cannot use contract information for purposes beyond legal verification of compliance with current law.\n\n## Worker Consent & Data Protection\n\nThe statute emphasizes that any data collection must respect:\n- Worker dignity and privacy (Article 18)\n- Applicable data protection law (referenced in Article 8.4)\n\nHowever, **the document contains no specific provisions on consent requirements for performance scoring, gamification systems, or algorithmic monitoring.**\n\n## Notable Absence\n\nArticles addressing \"gamification\" or performance-scoring systems are not present in this legislative text. {"parentUuid":"210cc2b7-033b-409a-a696-83c10f8318df","isSidechain":true,"promptId":"49f4c30e-a636-409b-aca9-0d3079f18ad7","agentId":"a3cb307856fb26fcd","type":"user","message":{"role":"user","content":[{"tool_use_id":"toolu_01CvWNpuDLECH7Q9wE9ff1hd","type":"tool_result","content":"# The Octalysis Framework: 8 Core Drives for Engagement\n\n## Overview\n\nThe Octalysis Framework is a behavioral design methodology developed by Yu-kai Chou that identifies eight fundamental human motivations. It emphasizes \"Human-Focused Design\" rather than function-focused approaches, helping organizations understand *why* people engage, not just *what* mechanics to deploy.\n\n## The 8 Core Drives\n\n| Drive | Focus | Workplace Application |\n|-------|-------|----------------------|\n| **Epic Meaning & Calling** | Feeling part of something greater | Frame roles as contributing to organizational mission |\n| **Development & Accomplishment** | Progress and overcoming challenges | Clear progression paths, skill-building opportunities |\n| **Empowerment of Creativity & Feedback** | Creative expression with feedback loops | Innovation challenges, collaborative projects |\n| **Ownership & Possession** | Sense of ownership | Personalized workspaces, career development plans |\n| **Social Influence & Relatedness** | Community and connection | Team collaboration, peer recognition programs |\n| **Scarcity & Impatience** | Wanting what's limited | Limited-time opportunities, exclusive access levels |\n| **Unpredictability & Curiosity** | Discovering what happens next | Surprise recognition, varied project assignments |\n| **Loss & Avoidance** | Avoiding negative outcomes | Streak tracking, performance incentives |\n\n## Implementation Mechanics\n\n**Points & Badges**: Track accomplishments tied to specific Core Drives (badges for development milestones, points for collaborative contributions)\n\n**Leaderboards**: Activate social influence through peer comparison (team rankings, peer recognition boards)\n\n**Streaks**: Leverage loss avoidance to maintain consistent engagement (daily participation chains, attendance records)\n\n**Unpredictability Elements**: Rotate recognition recipients, vary project types to maintain curiosity\n\n## White Hat vs. Black Hat Gamification\n\n**White Hat** (top four drives): Inspires autonomy and empowerment through Epic Meaning, Development, Empowerment, and Ownership.\n\n**Black Hat** (bottom four drives): Creates urgency through Scarcity, Unpredictability, and Loss Avoidance—effective but potentially manipulative.\n\n## Workplace Example\n\nA software company implements Octalysis by combining: mission-driven project framing (Epic Meaning), clear promotion criteria (Development), innovation hackathons (Empowerment), individual skill portfolios (Ownership), cross-team collaboration (Social Influence), limited training spots (Scarcity), rotating mentorship (Unpredictability), and performance streaks (Loss Avoidance)."}]},"uuid":"46d0d732-129b-482a-9403-6c3d0607f80f","timestamp":"2026-03-14T18:54:00.061Z","sourceToolAssistantUUID":"210cc2b7-033b-409a-a696-83c10f8318df","userType":"external","cwd":"/Users/lr0y/Movies/claude-quickstarts-main/grandcafe-cheers-platform/app/grandcafe-cheers-app","sessionId":"7ce55231-69c9-4cc3-ba3c-94e14e50c506","version":"2.1.76","gitBranch":"main","slug":"snoopy-cooking-sifakis"}

Let me now compile the comprehensive research report.\n\nHere is the comprehensive research report covering all 10 areas:\n\n---\n\n# Gamification & Employee Engagement Research for GrandCafe Cheers\n\n## Context Baseline: What You Already Have\n\nBefore recommending additions, here is what the existing Cheers platform already provides that serves as a foundation for gamification:\n\n- **Post-shift surveys** (`shift_survey_responses` table): 5-point emoji rating (1-5), free-text feedback, anomaly detection (overtime/undertime/break variance at 15min threshold), AI sentiment analysis, manager review workflow\n- **Training school (\"Cheers School\")**: 68 guides across 6 categories (Food Safety, Occupational Health, Labor Regulations, Role Specific, Required Docs, Environmental), test questions with passing scores, training records per employee, certificate generation (PDF), compliance dashboard with per-employee status tracking, assignment system with due dates\n- **Clock in/out system**: shift-linked time tracking, break tracking, variance calculation\n- **Employee profiles**: 7 roles (admin, owner, manager, kitchen, bar, waiter, dj), linked to Supabase auth\n- **Customer loyalty_rewards table**: visit milestones with rewards (exists but for customers, not staff)\n\nKey insight: you have the data infrastructure for training progress, shift behavior, and feedback already -- gamification layers on top of this existing data rather than requiring new data collection.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Gamification in Restaurant Apps -- What Exists (Real Implementations)\n\n### 7shifts (Industry Leader for Restaurant Scheduling)\nSource: 7shifts.com/employee-engagement\n\n**Real features:**\n- **Engagement Dashboard**: Aggregates data from schedule, time clock, shift pool. Tracks shift feedback scores, attendance metrics, no-shows, dropped shifts, and reliability rankings per employee.\n- **Shift Feedback System**: Automated post-shift surveys (your existing emoji survey is very similar). Managers get notifications 1-60 minutes before/after shifts, with 48-hour response windows.\n- **Performance Tracking**: Individual profiles compile attendance trends, punctuality data, engagement activity. Managers add coaching notes backed by actual data.\n- **Recognition**: Public acknowledgment of staff achievements within the app.\n- **Results**: 88% of teams report improved morale/retention/performance. 13% average increase in employee retention. 93% of teams resolve conflicts using shift feedback.\n\n**Relevance to Cheers**: Your shift survey system is already at parity with 7shifts. The gap is in the aggregation/dashboard layer -- turning individual survey responses into trend visualizations and reliability scores.\n\n### Connecteam (Deskless Worker Platform)\nConnecteam's recognition features for restaurants include:\n- **Token System**: Virtual currency (tokens) managers give employees, redeemable for gift cards (Amazon, etc.)\n- **Badges**: Custom digital badges for achievements\n- **Social Feed**: Company-wide recognition wall where shout-outs appear\n- **Training Gamification**: Quizzes with leaderboards, course completion tracking, micro-learning modules\n\n### HeyTaco (Peer Recognition, 67% Daily Active Rate)\nSource: heytaco.com\n\n**Real mechanics:**\n- Every team member gets 5 tacos daily to distribute as recognition\n- Daily cap prevents inflation and ensures selectivity\n- Public recognition in communication channels\n- Leaderboards celebrate both top givers AND receivers\n- Tacos redeemable for 2,000+ gift cards, extra PTO, premium parking, charity donations, or custom perks\n- Typical redemption rate: 1 taco = EUR 0.50\n- **67% daily active participation** vs 35-45% industry average\n- Integrates into Slack/Teams natively (no separate app)\n\n### What Restaurants Actually Gamify (from industry analysis)\nThe metrics that restaurants successfully gamify fall into these categories:\n\n| Category | Metrics | How Measured |\n|----------|---------|--------------|\n| Punctuality | On-time arrivals, no-shows | Clock-in data (you have this) |\n| Training | Completion rates, test scores, certifications | Training records (you have this) |\n| Shift quality | Post-shift ratings, anomaly-free shifts | Survey data (you have this) |\n| Upselling | Average ticket size, specific item sales | POS data (you have this in `sales`/`pos_transactions`) |\n| Attendance | Shift completion rate, swap frequency | Shift/clock data (you have this) |\n| Peer feedback | Recognition given/received | New feature needed |\n| Customer satisfaction | Review scores, repeat visits | CRM data (you have `reviews`, `customers`) |\n\n---\n\n## 2. Points & Rewards Systems That Work\n\n### Recommended XP System for Cheers\n\nBased on the Octalysis framework (Yu-kai Chou) and successful implementations like HeyTaco and 7shifts, here is a concrete point system:\n\n#### XP Earning Events (all computed from existing data)\n\n```\nSHIFT XP:\n  Complete a shift:                    +10 XP\n  On-time clock-in (within 5 min):     +5 XP\n  Positive shift rating (4-5 emoji):   +3 XP\n  No anomaly on shift:                 +2 XP\n  Weekend/holiday shift bonus:         +5 XP\n\nTRAINING XP:\n  Start a course:                      +5 XP\n  Complete a course:                   +15 XP\n  Pass test on first attempt:          +10 XP bonus\n  Score 90%+ on test:                  +5 XP bonus\n  Complete all courses in category:    +25 XP bonus\n\nSTREAK XP:\n  3-day on-time streak:                +10 XP\n  7-day on-time streak:                +25 XP\n  14-day on-time streak:               +50 XP\n  3 positive shifts in a row:          +15 XP\n\nSOCIAL XP:\n  Give a kudos:                        +2 XP\n  Receive a kudos:                     +3 XP\n  Help a colleague (manager-verified): +10 XP\n\nSEASONAL:\n  Complete first week:                 +50 XP\n  Complete first month:                +100 XP\n  Survive full season:                 +500 XP\n```\n\n#### Level Progression\n\n```\nLevel 1  \"Newbie\":         0 XP\nLevel 2  \"Regular\":        100 XP\nLevel 3  \"Reliable\":       300 XP\nLevel 4  \"Pro\":            600 XP\nLevel 5  \"Expert\":         1000 XP\nLevel 6  \"All-Star\":       1500 XP\nLevel 7  \"Legend\":         2500 XP\nLevel 8  \"Season Champion\": 4000 XP\n```\n\n#### Rewards That Convert (GDPR-safe, cost-effective for 20-30 staff)\n\n| XP Cost | Reward | Notes |\n|---------|--------|-------|\n| 200 | Free meal during shift | Near zero cost |\n| 300 | Shift preference for 1 week | Choose your schedule first |\n| 500 | Half-day off (manager approval) | Popular in seasonal work |\n| 750 | EUR 25 gift card | Budget-friendly |\n| 1000 | \"Employee of the Month\" parking | Free, high status |\n| 1500 | Early season end (leave 1 day early) | Seasonal-specific |\n| 2000 | Reference letter from owner | Career value, zero cost |\n\n#### Avoiding Toxic Competition\n\nKey design principles from research:\n- **No negative XP**: Never deduct points (this creates anxiety, not motivation)\n- **Personal progress over ranking**: Show \"You earned 45 XP this week, up from 30 last week\" not \"You are #12 out of 25\"\n- **Team XP pool**: A percentage of individual XP contributes to team goals (\"Bar team: 2,340/3,000 XP to unlock Friday team dinner\")\n- **Redemption is private**: Others see badges, not point balances\n- **No XP decay**: Once earned, XP stays (unlike Duolingo streaks that reset)\n\n---\n\n## 3. Badges & Achievements\n\n### Recommended Badge System\n\nOrganized by the Octalysis framework's \"Development & Accomplishment\" drive:\n\n#### Onboarding Badges (Earned once)\n```\n\"First Day\"          - Complete first shift\n\"Orientation Hero\"   - Complete all onboarding courses within first week\n\"Part of the Team\"   - Receive first kudos from a colleague\n\"Clock Master\"       - First on-time clock-in\n```\n\n#### Skill Badges (Training-linked, directly from Cheers School data)\n```\n\"HACCP Certified\"         - Pass Food Safety G-FS-001\n\"Allergen Expert\"         - Pass G-FS-006 (Allergen Management)\n\"Fire Safety Trained\"     - Pass G-LAB-003 (Fire Prevention)\n\"First Aid Ready\"         - Pass G-LAB-007\n\"Temperature Guardian\"    - Pass G-FS-003 (Temperature Control)\n\"Cleaning Champion\"       - Pass G-FS-005 (Cleaning & Disinfection)\n\"Waste Warrior\"           - Pass G-ENV-001 and G-ENV-002\n\"Full Compliance\"         - Complete ALL mandatory courses for your role\n```\n\n#### Performance Badges (Computed from existing data)\n```\n\"Punctuality Pro\"        - 20 consecutive on-time arrivals\n\"Shift Warrior\"          - 50 shifts completed\n\"Century Club\"           - 100 shifts completed\n\"Consistent Performer\"   - 10 consecutive 4+ star shift ratings\n\"Zero Anomaly Month\"     - Full calendar month without shift anomalies\n\"Weekend Warrior\"        - 10 weekend shifts completed\n\"Night Owl\"              - 20 evening shifts completed\n```\n\n#### Seasonal Badges (Cheers-specific)\n```\n\"Opening Night Hero\"      - Work opening night of season\n\"Summer Survivor\"         - Complete full July + August\n\"Season Finisher\"         - Work final night of season\n\"Full Season Champion\"    - Work from opening to closing\n\"Storm Trooper\"           - Work 3+ shifts during bad weather weeks\n```\n\n#### Social Badges\n```\n\"Team Player\"            - Receive 10 kudos\n\"Generous Spirit\"        - Give 50 kudos\n\"Mentor\"                 - Help 5 new employees (manager-verified)\n\"Most Appreciated\"       - Most kudos received in a week (3 times)\n```\n\n### Display Strategy\n- **Profile card**: Top 3 badges prominently displayed (user's choice)\n- **Badge wall**: Full collection viewable on profile, greyed-out silhouettes for unearned badges (creates aspiration)\n- **Certificate sharing**: Existing PDF certificate download already works; add WhatsApp/LinkedIn share buttons to `CertificateCard` component\n- **Physical element**: Print QR code linking to digital badge wall on employee name tag\n\n---\n\n## 4. Leaderboards -- Good vs Toxic\n\n### Research Findings\n\nFrom the Octalysis framework analysis, leaderboards activate \"Social Influence & Relatedness\" (White Hat, positive) but can slip into \"Loss & Avoidance\" (Black Hat, anxiety-inducing) if implemented poorly.\n\n**When leaderboards HELP:**\n- Small teams (under 30 -- your case)\n- When they rotate/reset weekly (not cumulative forever)\n- When they celebrate multiple dimensions (not just one metric)\n- When team-based, not purely individual\n- When top AND bottom are treated well (no public shaming)\n\n**When leaderboards HURT:**\n- Permanent rankings visible to all\n- Single-metric focus (e.g., only speed)\n- When bottom performers are visible and identifiable\n- When tied to compensation or termination decisions\n- When gaming is possible (and rewarded)\n\n### Recommended Implementation for Cheers\n\n#### 1. Weekly Highlights (Instead of Permanent Ranking)\n\n```\n\"This Week's Highlights\" (refreshes every Monday)\n- Most Kudos Received: Anna (12 kudos)\n- Training Star: Marco (completed 3 courses)\n- Punctuality Perfect: Lisa, Jan, Pedro (100% on-time)\n- Shift Streak: Ahmed (14 shifts without anomaly)\n```\n\nDisplay as a social feed/story format, not as a numbered list.\n\n#### 2. Department Challenges (Team-Based)\n\n```\n\"January Challenge: Training Sprint\"\n  Kitchen: 85% courses completed [===========   ]\n  Bar:     72% courses completed [=========     ]\n  Floor:   91% courses completed [============  ]\n\nWinning team gets: Team dinner on the house\n```\n\nThis activates friendly inter-department competition without individual shaming.\n\n#### 3. Personal Progress Dashboard (Private)\n\nOnly the individual employee sees:\n- Their XP trend over time (line chart)\n- \"Your best week: 95 XP\" personal records\n- Comparison to their own past performance (not others)\n- \"You're in the top 25% for punctuality this month\" (percentile, not rank)\n\n---\n\n## 5. Peer Recognition / Social Features\n\n### Recommended \"Kudos\" System\n\nBased on HeyTaco mechanics (67% daily engagement rate), adapted for a 20-30 person restaurant:\n\n#### Core Mechanics\n- Each employee gets **3 kudos per day** (not 5 -- smaller team needs less)\n- Kudos are **public** (visible on a team feed)\n- Each kudos has a **category tag**:\n  - \"Teamwork\" -- helped during a rush\n  - \"Going Extra\" -- stayed late, covered a gap\n  - \"Teaching\" -- showed a new person the ropes\n  - \"Positive Vibes\" -- kept energy up\n  - \"Customer Hero\" -- great customer interaction\n- Short message required (minimum 10 characters): \"Anna helped me when 3 tables came at once\"\n- **Manager kudos** are weighted 2x (but managers also only get 3/day)\n\n#### \"Employee of the Week\" (Automated)\nComputed weekly from:\n- Most kudos received (40% weight)\n- Highest average shift rating (30% weight)\n- Training progress (20% weight)\n- Punctuality score (10% weight)\n\nDisplayed prominently in app dashboard. Manager can override/adjust.\n\n#### Anonymous vs Public\n\nResearch finding: **Public praise works better than anonymous** in small teams. Anonymous feedback creates suspicion in tight-knit groups. The optimal approach:\n- **Kudos: Always public** with sender name visible\n- **Shift feedback: Always private** between employee and manager\n- **Improvement suggestions: Anonymous option available** (via the existing survey free-text field)\n\n---\n\n## 6. Training School Integration (Cheers School Gamification)\n\nYour training system already has strong bones. Here are specific enhancements:\n\n### Visual Learning Paths / Skill Trees\n\nMap the 6 categories as a visual tree with dependencies:\n\n```\nFOOD SAFETY PATH (22 guides)\n  Tier 1 (Required First):\n    G-FS-001 (HACCP Basics) ──→ G-FS-002 (Hygiene)\n                              └→ G-FS-005 (Cleaning)\n  Tier 2 (Unlocked after Tier 1):\n    G-FS-003 (Temperature) ──→ G-FS-004 (Food Storage)\n    G-FS-006 (Allergens)\n  Tier 3 (Advanced):\n    G-FS-017 (Kitchen Safety) ── Requires: G-FS-003 + G-FS-004\n```\n\nYour `relatedCodes` field in `GuideMetadata` already defines these relationships. The skill tree visualization reads from this data.\n\n### Training Streaks\n\nLeverage \"Loss & Avoidance\" drive (Octalysis Drive #8):\n- \"Study streak\": Complete at least 1 section of any course per day\n- Visual: flame icon with day count\n- Streak freeze: 1 per week (earned at 7+ day streak) -- prevents frustration\n- No permanent loss -- streak just resets, XP already earned stays\n\n### Micro-Learning (Daily 2-Min Tips)\n\nPush notification with a single fact/question from existing course content:\n- \"Quick Quiz: At what temperature must you store raw chicken? [Tap to answer]\"\n- Source questions from `training_test_questions` table\n- One push notification per day at 10:00 AM (before shifts start)\n- Answering correctly earns 2 XP\n- Wrong answer links to the relevant course section\n\n### Team Training Challenges\n\nComputed from `training_assignments` and `training_records`:\n```\n\"Bar Team Challenge: All certified by June 15\"\n  Progress: 4/6 members completed\n  Time left: 8 days\n  Reward: Team breakfast + 50 XP each\n```\n\n### Certificate Sharing Enhancement\n\nYour `CertificateCard` component already generates certificates. Add:\n- WhatsApp share button (deep link: `whatsapp://send?text=I just earned my HACCP certification!`)\n- LinkedIn share (Open Graph image of the certificate)\n- Instagram Story template (branded Cheers frame around certificate)\n- In-app celebration animation when test is passed (confetti burst, 2 seconds)\n\n### Progress Bar on Profile\n\nComputed from `TrainingComplianceStats` (already exists in your types):\n```\nTraining Progress: 14/22 required courses completed [64%]\n███████████░░░░░░ \n\nNext up: G-FS-011 (Kitchen Equipment Cleaning)\n```\n\n---\n\n## 7. Shift Experience Gamification\n\n### Enhancing the Existing Post-Shift Survey\n\nYour emoji survey already tracks mood (1-5 rating). Layer on:\n\n#### \"Personal Best\" Tracking\nComputed from `shift_survey_responses`:\n```\nYour Stats:\n  Current positive streak: 7 shifts (personal best: 12)\n  Average rating this month: 4.2 (up from 3.8 last month)\n  Shifts completed: 42 this season\n```\n\n#### Milestone Celebrations\nTriggered by count queries on `clock_in_out`:\n```\n\"This was your 50th shift at Cheers! 🎉\"\n\"You've worked 200 hours this season!\"\n\"You've completed your 10th weekend shift!\"\n```\n\nShow as a modal overlay after clock-out, before the survey prompt.\n\n#### Team Shift Score\nComputed daily from all survey responses:\n```\n\"Today's team vibe: 4.1/5 ⭐\"\n  Kitchen: 4.3  |  Bar: 4.0  |  Floor: 3.9\n  Yesterday: 3.8 | Week avg: 4.0\n```\n\nVisible on the dashboard, creates shared ownership of the work atmosphere.\n\n#### Shift Quality Score (Private, per employee)\nComposite score visible only to the employee and their manager:\n```\nShift Quality = (\n  punctuality_score * 0.3 +     // from clock_in variance\n  break_compliance * 0.2 +       // from break_variance_minutes\n  shift_rating * 0.3 +           // from survey rating\n  anomaly_free * 0.2              // boolean from anomaly_type\n) * 100\n```\n\n---\n\n## 8. GDPR Considerations for Employee Gamification in EU/Spain\n\n### Legal Framework\n\nThree laws govern this:\n\n1. **GDPR** (EU-wide): General principles\n2. **LOPDGDD** (Spain's GDPR implementation, Ley Organica 3/2018): Spain-specific rules\n3. **Estatuto de los Trabajadores** (Workers' Statute, Royal Decree 2/2015): Labor-specific rights\n\n### What You CAN Track (Lawful Basis: Legitimate Interest or Contract)\n\n| Data | Lawful Basis | Notes |\n|------|-------------|-------|\n| Clock-in/out times | Employment contract | Already collected |\n| Training completion | Legal obligation (HACCP, fire safety are legally required) | Already collected |\n| Shift survey ratings | Legitimate interest | Already collected, employee-submitted |\n| Badges earned | Legitimate interest | Derived from above data |\n| XP points | Legitimate interest | Derived from above data |\n| Kudos given/received | Consent | New data, requires explicit opt-in |\n\n### What Requires EXPLICIT Consent (Article 6 LOPDGDD)\n\n- **Peer-to-peer recognition/kudos**: New data collection about interpersonal relationships\n- **Leaderboard visibility**: Making individual performance data visible to peers\n- **Badge sharing externally**: Sharing training certificates on social media\n- **Profile photos on achievement displays**: Using likeness in gamification\n\n### What You CANNOT Do\n\n- **Gamification as performance evaluation tool for termination decisions**: Article 20.3 ET allows monitoring but LOPDGDD Article 28.2(d) requires DPIA (Data Protection Impact Assessment) for profiling-based decisions affecting employees\n- **Mandatory participation in social features**: Kudos, leaderboards must be opt-in\n- **Track location/movement patterns**: Beyond clock-in/out point\n- **Use AI to profile employees for hiring/firing**: GDPR Article 22 restricts automated decision-making\n\n### Required Steps Before Launch\n\n1. **Data Protection Impact Assessment (DPIA)**: Required under LOPDGDD Article 28.2(d) because gamification involves \"evaluation of personal aspects\" -- specifically work performance analysis. Must be documented before going live.\n\n2. **Employee Information Notice**: Written document explaining:\n   - What gamification data is collected\n   - How XP/badges are calculated\n   - Who sees what (manager vs peers vs public)\n   - Right to opt out of social features\n   - Right to access, correct, and delete their data\n   - Data retention period (recommend: delete 6 months after season ends)\n\n3. **Works Council Notification**: Under Article 64.5 of the Estatuto de los Trabajadores, the comite de empresa (if one exists, required for businesses with 50+ employees) must be informed about monitoring systems. With 20-30 employees, you likely have delegados de personal (employee delegates) instead. They should be informed, though formal consultation is not legally required under 50 employees.\n\n4. **Consent Collection**: In-app consent flow at first login:\n   ```\n   \"Cheers uses a gamification system to make your work more engaging.\n    - Your shift data and training progress earn XP points and badges\n    - You can optionally participate in peer kudos and team leaderboards\n    \n    [x] I understand how my data is used (required)\n    [ ] I want to participate in kudos and leaderboards (optional)\n    \n    You can change these settings anytime in your profile.\"\n   ```\n\n5. **Data Retention**: Delete all gamification data (XP, badges, kudos) within 6 months of employment end, per data minimization principles. Training compliance records may be retained longer if legally required (HACCP records: 5 years).\n\n### Risk: Gamification as Surveillance\n\nThe key GDPR risk is perception. Article 89 of LOPDGDD and Article 20.3 of the Workers' Statute both require that monitoring \"maintain dignity and consideration due to the worker.\" Design principle: **gamification should feel like a reward system, not a monitoring system**. This means:\n- Employees control their own profile visibility\n- No negative consequences for low XP\n- Managers see aggregated trends, not real-time individual tracking\n- Participation in social features is always voluntary\n\n---\n\n## 9. UX Patterns for Gamification in Mobile\n\n### Where Points/Badges Appear (Without Clutter)\n\n```\nMAIN NAVIGATION (unchanged):\n  Dashboard | Schedule | Training | Chat | Profile\n                                            ↑ Badge count dot\n\nDASHBOARD (add one card):\n  [Existing cards: Today's Shift, Clock In/Out, etc.]\n  [NEW: \"Your Progress\" card]\n    Level 4 \"Pro\" | 623/1000 XP to next level\n    ████████████░░░ 62%\n    🔥 7-day streak | 3 badges this week\n\nPROFILE SCREEN (enhanced):\n  [Photo, Name, Role]\n  [XP Bar: Level 4 Pro - 623 XP]\n  [Top 3 Badges: HACCP | Punctuality Pro | Team Player]\n  [View All Badges →]\n  [This Week: +45 XP]\n  [Training: 14/22 complete]\n\nTRAINING SCREEN (enhanced):\n  [Add skill tree visualization at top]\n  [Add \"Daily Quiz\" card]\n  [Add streak counter]\n```\n\n### Notification Strategy\n\nBased on Duolingo's research (which found that well-timed notifications are the single biggest driver of streak retention):\n\n| Trigger | Notification | Frequency Cap |\n|---------|-------------|---------------|\n| Badge earned | \"You just earned 'Punctuality Pro'!\" | Immediate, max 2/day |\n| Level up | \"Level up! You're now a Pro (Level 4)\" | When it happens |\n| Streak at risk | \"Your 7-day streak! Complete today's quiz to keep it\" | 1/day max, 10 AM |\n| Kudos received | \"Anna gave you kudos: 'Great teamwork tonight!'\" | Batch at end of shift |\n| Milestone | \"50 shifts completed! You're a Cheers veteran\" | When it happens |\n| Weekly summary | \"Last week: +45 XP, 2 badges, 3 kudos received\" | Monday 9 AM |\n\n**Never notify about:**\n- Other people's achievements (avoid comparison anxiety)\n- Low scores or declining metrics\n- Missed streaks (just let them reset quietly)\n\n### Celebration Animations\n\nUse React Native Reanimated or Lottie for:\n- **Badge earned**: Badge icon drops from top, slight bounce, glow effect (1.5 sec)\n- **Level up**: Background color pulse, level number counts up, XP bar fills (2 sec)\n- **Milestone**: Confetti burst from bottom (react-native-confetti-cannon or custom), 2 sec\n- **Streak**: Flame icon grows slightly, number increments\n- **Test passed**: Checkmark draws itself, certificate slides in\n\nKeep ALL animations under 3 seconds. Add haptic feedback (light tap) on badge earn.\n\n### Social Feed\n\nDedicated tab or section in dashboard:\n```\nTEAM FEED (opt-in only)\n  🏆 Marco earned \"HACCP Certified\" badge        2h ago\n  👏 Anna → Pedro: \"Covered my break perfectly\"   3h ago\n  🎯 Kitchen team: 85% training complete!         5h ago\n  🔥 Lisa hit a 14-day punctuality streak!        1d ago\n```\n\nThis is public but curated: only positive events appear. No \"Pedro was late\" or \"Low rating\" entries.\n\n---\n\n## 10. ROI of Gamification in Restaurants\n\n### Research Data\n\n**Gallup Meta-Analysis (456 studies, 2.7M employees):**\n- Top-quartile engaged teams vs bottom-quartile:\n  - 18% higher sales productivity\n  - 81% lower absenteeism\n  - 18-43% lower turnover\n  - 64% fewer safety incidents\n  - 23% higher profitability\n- \"Managers account for 70% of the variance in team-level engagement\"\n\n**TalentLMS Survey (2019, gamification-specific):**\n- 89% of employees report gamification makes them more productive\n- 88% say gamification makes them happier\n- 83% of those receiving gamified training feel motivated\n- 61% of those receiving NON-gamified training feel \"bored and unproductive\"\n- Training completion rates increase 40-60% with gamification\n\n**HeyTaco:**\n- 67% daily active participation (vs 35-45% for typical recognition programs)\n\n### Projected ROI for a 20-30 Person Seasonal Restaurant\n\n**Costs:**\n- Development time: ~80-120 hours to build core gamification features\n- Gift card rewards budget: EUR 50-100/month (if using real rewards)\n- Ongoing: near-zero (automated, computed from existing data)\n\n**Expected Benefits (conservative estimates):**\n\n| Metric | Current (Est.) | With Gamification | Impact |\n|--------|---------------|-------------------|--------|\n| Training completion rate | 60-70% | 85-95% | Legal compliance + better service |\n| Punctuality (on-time %) | 80-85% | 90-95% | Fewer rush-hour gaps |\n| Seasonal retention | Staff leave mid-season | 15-25% fewer mid-season departures | Major cost saving (recruiting + training replacement = EUR 2,000-3,000 per person) |\n| Post-shift survey response rate | 40-60% | 70-85% | Better data for management |\n| Time to full proficiency | 3-4 weeks | 2-3 weeks | Faster seasonal ramp-up |\n\n**Metrics the Owner Should Track:**\n\n1. **Engagement Rate**: % of employees who interact with gamification features weekly (target: 60%+)\n2. **Training Velocity**: Average days from assignment to completion (should decrease)\n3. **Punctuality Trend**: % on-time arrivals month-over-month\n4. **Retention Rate**: Mid-season departure rate compared to previous seasons\n5. **Survey Response Rate**: % of shifts that get a post-shift survey response\n6. **Kudos Activity**: Average kudos given per person per week (healthy: 2-4)\n7. **NPS from Staff**: Add one question quarterly: \"Would you recommend working at Cheers?\"\n\n---\n\n## Summary: Implementation Priority Matrix\n\n| Feature | Effort | Impact | Leverage Existing Data? | Priority |\n|---------|--------|--------|------------------------|----------|\n| XP system (computed from shifts + training) | Medium | High | Yes -- clock_in_out, training_records, shift_surveys | P1 |\n| Badge system (achievement definitions) | Low | High | Yes -- all derived from existing tables | P1 |\n| Training skill tree visualization | Low | Medium | Yes -- push | Medium | Medium | Yes -- training_test_questions | P2 |\n| Team challenges | Medium | Medium | Aggregation on existing data | P3 |\n| Social feed | Medium | Medium | New + aggregation | P3 |\n| Reward redemption shop | Medium | Low-Medium | New table needed | P3 |\n| GDPR consent flow | Low | Critical | Must do before launch | P0 |\n\n### Database Tables Needed\n\nFor the new features, you need approximately 5 new tables:\n\n```sql\n-- Gamification core\nemployee_xp_events       -- individual XP earning events (audit trail)\nemployee_badges          -- earned badges with timestamps\nemployee_streaks         -- current streak tracking\n\n-- Social features\nkudos                    -- peer recognition entries\ngamification_consent     -- GDPR consent records per employee\n```\n\nAll XP totals, levels, and leaderboard positions should be **computed views** (Supabase materialized views or computed at query time), not stored state -- this keeps the system immutable and
